jane goodall helps humans and animals live together	珍•古拉爾幫助人類和動物一起生活在一起 ,
good afternoon , good evening , whatever .	午安 , 晚安 , 等等 。
we can go , jambo , guten abend , bonsoir , but we can also ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh .	我們能去 , 賈莫 , 吉姆.阿伯丁 , 波諾 , 但我們也可以 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 喔 , 哦 。
that is the call that chimpanzees make before they go to sleep in the evening .	這就是黑猩猩在晚上睡覺之前所接到的電話 。
you hear it going from one side of the valley to the other , from one group of nests to the next .	你聽到它從山谷的一邊傳到另一邊 , 從一群的巢穴傳到下一邊 。
and i want to pick up with my talk this evening from where zeray left off yesterday .	今天晚上 , 我想要帶著我的演說 , 從昨天zeray離開的地方 。
he was talking about this amazing , threeyearold australopithecine child , selam .	他在談的是這個奇妙的三歲大的澳大利亞小孩 , selam 。
and we've also been hearing about the history , the family tree , of mankind through dna genetic profiling .	我們也聽過人類的歷史、家譜、人類透過基因檔案來獲取 。
and it was a paleontologist , the late louis leakey , who actually set me on the path for studying chimpanzees .	這是一位古生物學家 , 已故路易斯•萊基 , 他讓我踏上了研究黑猩猩的路 。
and it was pretty extraordinary , way back then .	當時是非常不凡的 。
it's kind of commonplace now , but his argument was because he'd been searching for the fossilized remains of early humans in africa .	現在有點常見 , 但他的論點是 , 因為他一直在尋找非洲早期人類的化石 。
and you can tell an awful lot about what those beings looked like from the fossils , from the shape of the muscle attachments , something about the way they lived from the various artifacts found with them .	從化石的形狀 , 你可以分辨出很多的生物 , 從肌肉依附的形狀 , 從不同文物中 , 牠們是怎麼生活的 。
but what about how they behaved ? that's what he wanted to know .	但他們的行為如何呢 ? 這是他想要知道的 。
and of course , behavior doesn't fossilize .	當然 , 行為並沒有化石 。
he argued and it's now a fairly common theory that if we found behavior patterns similar or the same in our closest living relatives , the great apes , and humans today , then maybe those behaviors were present in the apelike , humanlike ancestor some seven million years ago .	他主張 , 現在是一個相當常見的理論 , 如果我們在最接近的生物親戚身上找到行為模式 , 或類似的行為模式 , 如今人類 , 也許這些行為在大約七百萬年前就出現了 , 人類的祖先 。
and therefore , perhaps we had brought those characteristics with us from that ancient , ancient past .	因此 , 也許我們把這些特徵從古代、古代的過去帶給了我們 。
well , if you look in textbooks today that deal with human evolution , you very often find people speculating about how early humans may have behaved , based on the behavior of chimpanzees .	嗯 , 如果你現在在教科書上看到處理人類演化的過程 , 你常常會發現人們在推測早期人類的行為 , 基於黑猩猩的行為 。
they are more like us than any other living creature , and we've heard about that during this ted conference .	牠們比其他生物更像我們 , 在ted的會議中 , 我們聽說過這件事 。
so it remains for me to comment on the ways in which chimpanzees are so like us , in certain aspects of their behavior .	所以 , 我一直在評論黑猩猩在某些方面和我們很相似的行為方式 。
every chimpanzee has his or her own personality .	每隻黑猩猩都有牠或牠自己的個性 。
of course , i gave them names . they can live to be 60 years or more , although we think most of them probably don't make it to 60 in the wild .	當然 , 我給了他們名字 。 他們可以活到六十年以上 , 雖然我們認為大部分的人可能不會在野外60歲 。
mr . wurzel . the female has her first baby when she's 11 or 12 .	女生在11或12歲時 , 她的第一個寶寶 。
thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	在那裡 , 她只有五、六年的嬰兒 , 一個長期的兒童依賴度 , 當孩子在晚上護理母親時 , 和她一起睡覺 , 背上騎著 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信 , 長期的童年期對黑猩猩來說很重要 , 就如同對我們而言 , 與學習有關 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	隨著大腦在不同形式的動物進化過程中變得更複雜 , 所以我們發現 , 學習在個人的生命史中扮演著更重要的角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕的黑猩猩花了很多時間看他們的長輩怎麼做 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	我們現在知道他們有能力模仿他們所看到的行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信 , 這種方式 , 目前在非洲各個黑猩猩族群中 , 所看到的各種不同的工具行為 , 都在研究這些行為 , 如何從一個世代傳到下一個世代 , 透過觀察、模仿和實踐 , 這樣我們就能把這些工具行為描述成原始文化 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩沒有口語 , 我們已經談過了 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	他們的確有非常豐富的姿勢和姿勢 , 當中許多都很類似 , 甚至相同 , 和我們在同一個情境下形成 。 打招呼黑猩猩擁抱 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	他們也親吻、握手、拍手 。
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	他們搖擺 , 扔石頭 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩猩社會中 , 我們發現許多關於同情心的例子 , 前導者要愛和真正利他主義 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們和我們一樣 , 對他們的本質有著黑暗的一面 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	他們有能力極度殘酷 , 甚至是一種原始的戰爭 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些極具侵略性的行為 , 大部分是被指導對抗鄰近社群的個體 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	他們非常積極地激進 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	我相信 , 比起其他生物 , 黑猩猩已經幫助我們了解到 , 畢竟 , 人類和其他動物王國之間沒有尖銳的界線 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	這條線非常模糊 , 每當我們做更多觀察時 , 它就會變得越來越模糊 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我從1960年開始的研究仍然持續到今日 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	這些黑猩猩 , 在野外過著複雜的社交生活 , 協助了我們了解到我們是其中的一部分 , 而不是和我們共享地球的神奇動物分開來的 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	很遺憾 , 發現黑猩猩 , 就像世界上許多其他生物一樣 , 正在失去牠們的棲息地 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這只是一張從空中拍攝的照片 , 它顯示了戈柏的森林高地 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	那時我在整個地區飛越 , 大約16年前 , 我發現 , 在公園之外 , 這片森林 , 在1960年時幾乎沒有破裂 , 沿著坦尚尼卡湖的東岸 , 也就是小小的三十平方英雄的羊公園 , 這個問題來了我的腦海 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們要如何拯救這些知名的黑猩猩 , 當住在國家公園附近的人掙扎生存時 ? 」
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多人住在那裏 , 比那塊土地能支援的還要多 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	難民從緬甸湧入的數字增加 , 和剛果湖邊的數量 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	非常貧窮的人負擔不起從別處購買食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	這導致了一個計畫 , 我們稱它為tacare 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	這是一種非常全面的方式來改善人們生活在公園附近的村莊 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從十二個村莊開始 , 現在已經24個了 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時間深入探究它 , 但它包括樹木護士 , 目前最適合耕種的方法 , 幾乎像沙漠一樣落在這些山上 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	控制的方式 , 防止土壤侵蝕 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	再利用過度使用的農地 , 這樣兩年內 , 農地就能再次有生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	協助村民從井裡取得淡水 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	也許建造一些學校 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 與一小群女性合作 , 提供她們機會給微型貸款 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	如同世界各地的案例 , 我們有95%的貸款回報 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦權女性 , 與教育合作 , 為女孩們提供獎學金 , 讓他們能完成中學 , 清楚了解到 , 世界各地 , 身為女性的教育改善 , 家庭大小下降 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭規劃和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	由於這個計畫 , 有些事正在進行保育 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	保育的情況是 , 住在這24個村莊的農夫 , 與其把我們當成一群白人來研究一群猴子 , 順便一提 , 許多員工現在是坦尚尼亞人 , 但當我們開始了坦尚尼亞計劃時 , 是一個坦尚尼亞團隊進入村落 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	那是一位坦尚尼亞團隊和村民談話 , 問他們對什麼感興趣 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們對保育有興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對教育有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間過去 , 隨著情況開始改善 , 他們開始更了解保育的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解 , 隨著山丘的上層是樹木 , 所以你有這種可怕的土壤侵蝕和泥塊 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	現今 , 我們正在發展所謂的 「 更大的羊生態系統 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是一個遠離國家公園的區域 , 延伸到這些非常退化的土地上 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	當這些村莊有更好的生活標準時 , 他們其實同意把百分之十到二十的高地放到一旁 , 這樣一來 , 當樹木長回來時 , 黑猩猩就會有葉面的走廊 , 可以在國家公園以外的遺傳村莊和其他殘留的遺傳團體互動 。
so tacare is a success .	所以 , 坦尚是成功的 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們在非洲其它地方複製它 , 在其他地方 , 面臨極端人口壓力的荒野區域 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 非洲的問題 , 正如我們在ted的前幾天所討論的 , 都是重大的問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	有很大的貧窮 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	當你收到大量住在土地上的人 , 那不是肥沃 , 尤其是當你砍掉樹木 , 你把土壤留在侵蝕的風上 , 因為絕望的人口減少了越來越多的樹木 , 所以他們可以試著為自己和家人種植食物 , 會發生什麼事 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	其他問題不只在非洲 , 還在開發中國家的其他國家 , 不論在哪裡 , 我們在地球上做什麼 ?
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	你知道的 , 著名的科學家 , e.o.wilson說如果這個星球上每一個人都活在歐洲人或美國人的平均生活水準 , 我們需要三個新的行星 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	現今 , 他們說的是四個 。 但我們沒有 。 我們只有一個 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	到底發生了什麼事 ? 我的意思是 , 問題來了 , 我們是最聰明的生物 , 能夠走過地球 , 帶著非凡的腦袋 , 能夠用這些ted會議所描繪出來的科技 , 但我們卻在摧毀我們唯一的家園 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	世界各地的原住民 , 在他們做出重大決策之前 , 曾經坐下來問自己: 「 這個決策如何影響我們前面的七代人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要的決策 , 我不是特別在談非洲 , 而是已開發國家的主要決策 , 包含了數百萬美金 , 數百萬人 , 通常基於 「 這會如何影響下股東會議 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決定會影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我開始在非洲四處旅行 , 談到黑猩猩所面臨的問題 , 以及消失的森林 , 我了解到 , 非洲有多少問題可能是前次殖民地剝削 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以我開始到非洲外面去 , 在歐洲 , 說話 , 在美國說話 , 去亞洲 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	到處都有這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	你知道我在說的那種 。 我在說的是污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸的空氣通常會毒害我們 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球正在毒害我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水資源可能是這世紀我們要面對的最關鍵議題之一 , 到處都是農業、工業和家庭的污染 , 仍然被全世界噴灑的化學物質之一 , 似乎無法從過去經驗中獲利 。
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	紅樹林被砍伐 , 海嘯的效應變得更糟 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談過土壤侵蝕 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們有無數的燃燒化石燃料和其他溫室氣體一起燃燒 , 所以 , 稱為氣候變遷 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 全世界的人開始相信氣候有問題 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	全世界的氣候都被混合在一起 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	影響更糟的是窮人 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經受到影響 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在撒哈拉以南非洲的許多地區 , 乾旱越來越嚴重 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨來臨時 , 通常會導致洪水、加上苦難 , 以及貧窮、飢餓和疾病的循環 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	住在一個土地無法支撐的地區 , 太貧窮的人們無法購買食物 , 因為整個土地已經退化了 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以你會得到沙漠化、磨損、磨損 , 隨著樹木的最後一棵被砍伐 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這種事情不只發生在非洲 , 全世界都是如此 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以 , 我並不意外 , 當我在世界各地旅行時 , 我遇到了許多年輕人 , 他們似乎失去了希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去了智慧 , 原住民的智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問了一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	嗯 , 你認為在這個非凡聰明的大腦中 , 可能有某種區別 , 這種區分了ted的科技 , 而人類的心 ? 以科學的角度來說 , 在愛和同情的角度來說 , 是否有某種隔閡 ?
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	而這些年輕人 , 當我跟他們說話時 , 基本上他們不是憂鬱、冷漠、憤怒 , 他們說了同樣的話: 「 我們覺得你已經犯下了我們的未來 , 我們沒有辦法做這件事 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們已經妥協了他們的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小孫子 , 每當我看著他們 , 我想我們如何傷害這個美麗的星球 , 自從我年紀開始 , 我感到絕望 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	導致這個計畫 , 我們稱之為根與芽 , 它從坦尚尼亞開始 , 現在已經擴散到全世界97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是象徵性的 。 根是建立一間公司基礎 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	射擊看起來很小 ; 為了抵達太陽 , 它們可以穿過磚牆 。
see the brick wall as all these problems we've inflicted on the planet , environmental and social . it's a message of hope .	把磚牆看成我們在地球上所遇到的問題 , 環境和社會問題 。 這是希望的訊息 。
hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數十萬名年輕人可以打破這個世界 , 為所有生物創造一個更好的世界 。
the most important message of roots and shoots: every single one of us makes a difference , every single day .	根與芽的最重要的訊息:我們每一個人每天都能做出改變 。
we have a choice . every one of us in this room , we have a choice as to what kind of difference we want to make .	我們有選擇 。 在座的每一個人 , 我們都有選擇 , 我們想要做出什麼樣的差別 。
the very poor have no choice . it's up to us to change things so that the poor have choice as well .	窮人沒有選擇權 , 我們要改變現狀 , 讓窮人也有選擇 。
the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根與芽團體都選擇了三個計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	這取決於他們有多老 , 哪個國家 , 不論他們身在城市或鄉村 , 都要看什麼樣的計畫 。
but basically , we have programs now from preschool right through university , with more and more adults starting their own roots and shoots groups .	但基本上 , 我們現在已經從幼稚園到大學 , 越來越多的成人開始自己的根與芽團體 。
and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每個團體都選擇 , 在他們之間 , 三個不同的項目 , 來讓這個更美好的世界變得更好 , 了解到 , 所有這些不同的問題都互相連結 , 並互相影響 。
so one of their projects will be to help their own human community .	其中一項計畫就是幫助他們自己的社群 。
and then , if they're able , they may raise money to help communities in other parts of the world .	如果他們能夠的話 , 他們可能會籌錢協助世界其他地方的社區 。
one of their projects will be to help animals not just wildlife , domestic animals as well .	其中一項計畫是幫助動物 , 不僅僅是野生動物 , 家庭的動物 。
and one of their projects will be to help the environment that we all share .	其中一項計畫就是幫助我們共享的環境 。
and woven throughout all of this is a message of learning to live in peace and harmony within ourselves , in our families , in our communities , between nations , between cultures , between religions and between us and the natural world .	整體來說 , 學習在我們自己、在我們的家庭、在我們的社區、文化、宗教、我們之間、和自然界之間生活的訊息 。
we need the natural world . we cannot go on destroying it at the rate we are .	我們需要自然世界 。 我們不能以我們現在的速度去摧毀它 。
we not do have more than this one planet .	我們沒有比這個星球還多 。
just picking one or two of the projects right here in africa that the roots and shoots groups are doing , one or two projects only in tanzania , in uganda , kenya , south africa , congobrazzaville , sierra leone , cameroon and other groups . and as i say , it's in 97 countries around the world .	在非洲這裡挑選一到兩項項項目:根與芽團體正在進行 , 一到兩項專案只有在坦尚尼亞、肯亞、南非、剛果巴拉斯維爾、獅子山共和國、喀麥隆和其他團體 。 如我所說 , 它在世界上97個國家 。
of course , they're planting trees . they're growing organic vegetables .	當然 , 他們種植樹木 , 種植有機蔬菜 。
they're working in the refugee camps , with chickens and selling the eggs for a little amount of money , or just using them to feed their families , and feeling a sense of pride and empowerment , because they're no longer helpless and depending on others with their vegetables and their chickens .	他們在難民營工作 , 賣掉雞蛋 , 賣掉一些錢 , 或只用它們餵飽家人 , 感受到驕傲和賦權 , 因為他們不再無助 , 也不再仰賴其他人 , 他們的蔬菜和雞 。
it's being used in uganda to give some psychological help to exchild soldiers .	它被用在烏干達 , 給予一些心理協助 , 來展現士兵 。
doing projects like this is bringing them out of themselves .	做像這樣的計畫 , 把他們自己帶出去 。
once again , they're useful members of society .	再一次 , 他們是社會中有用的成員 。
we have this program in prisons as well .	我們在監獄也有這個計畫 。
so , there's no time for more roots and shoots now .	所以 , 現在沒有時間可以讓更多的根與芽 。
but oh , they're also working on hiv/aids .	但喔 , 他們也在研究hiv/aids 。
that's a very important component of roots and shoots , with older kids talking to younger ones .	這是根與芽的重要成分 , 與較年長的孩子對話 。
and unwanted pregnancies and things like that , which young people listen to better from other youth , rather than adults .	不想懷孕 , 諸如此類 , 年輕人會傾聽其他年輕人的聲音 , 而非成人 。
hope . that's the question i get asked as i'm going around the world: " jane , you've seen so many terrible things , you've seen your chimpanzees decrease in number from about one million , at the turn of the century , to no more than 150 , 000 now , and the same with so many other animals .	希望 。 這就是我在世界各地被問到的問題: 「 珍 , 你見過這麼多可怕的事情 , 你見過你的黑猩猩數量從一百萬增加到一世紀 , 到現在都不超過十五萬 , 其他動物也一樣 。
forests disappearing , deserts where once there was forest .	森林消失 , 曾經有森林的沙漠 。
do you really have hope ? " well , yes .	你真的有希望嗎 ? 」 好吧 。
you can't come to a conference like ted and not have hope , can you ?	你不能來參加像ted這樣的會議 , 沒有希望 , 你能嗎 ?
and of course , there's hope . one is this amazing human brain .	當然 , 還有希望 。 其中一個是人類的神奇大腦 。
and i mean , think of the technologies .	我的意思是 , 想想科技 。
and i've just been so thrilled , finally , to come to people talking about compost latrines .	最後 , 我很興奮 , 最後 , 來談談堆肥式廁所 。
it's one of my hobbyhorses .	它是我的嗜好之一 。
we just flush all this water down the lavatory , it's terrible .	我們只是把所有的水沖到火車上 , 很糟糕 。
and then talking about renewable energy desperately important .	接著 , 談論再生能源 , 極其重要 。
do we care about the planet for our children ?	我們是否在乎我們的孩子 ?
how many of us have children or grandchildren , nieces , nephews ?	有多少人有小孩或孫子、姪子、姪子 ?
do we care about their future ?	我們關心他們的未來嗎 ?
and if we care about their future , we , as the elite around the world , we can do something about it . we can make choices as to how we live each day .	如果我們關心他們的未來 , 我們 , 身為世界各地菁英 , 我們能做點什麼 。 我們可以做出選擇 , 來當我們每天的生活 。
what we buy . what we wear .	我們買了什麼 , 穿什麼 。
and choose to make these choices with the question , how will this affect the environment around me ?	選擇用問題來做這些選擇 , 這會如何影響我周圍的環境 ?
how will it affect the life of my child when he or she grows up ?	在他長大後 , 它會如何影響我的孩子的生活 ?
or my grandchild , or whatever it is .	或我的孫子 , 或其他東西 。
so the human brain , coupled with the human heart , and we join hands around the world .	所以 , 人類的大腦 , 和人類的心情結合 , 我們加入了全世界的手 。
and that's what ted is helping so well with , and google who help us , and esri are helping us with mapping in gombe national park .	ted就是這樣幫助我們 , 谷歌幫助我們 , esri也幫助我們繪製在gombe國家公園的地圖 。
all of these technologies we can use .	所有我們能使用的科技 。
now let's link them , and it's beginning to happen , isn't it ?	現在讓我們連結它們 , 開始發生了 , 不是嗎 ?
you've heard about it this afternoon . it's beginning to happen .	今天下午你已經聽過了 , 開始發生了 。
this change , this change . to see change that we must have if we care about the future .	這個改變 , 這個改變 。 若我們關心未來 , 我們必須要有所改變 。
and the next reason for hope nature is amazingly resilient .	希望大自然的下一個理由非常有韌性 。
you can take an area that's absolutely destroyed , with time and perhaps some help it can regenerate .	你可以把一個絕對被摧毀的區域 , 用時間 , 或許有些幫助它再生 。
and an example is the tacare program .	一個例子是坦尚尼亞計劃 。
i told you , where a seemingly dead tree stump if you stop hacking them for firewood , which you don't need to because you have wood lots , then in five years you can have a 30foot tree .	我告訴各位 , 看似死掉的樹木 , 如果你停止砍掉它們 , 你不需要砍掉它們 , 因為你有木頭 , 那麼五年內 , 你就有一棵30英呎樹 。
and animals , almost on the brink of extinction , can be given a second chance . that's my next book .	動物 , 幾乎在滅絕的邊緣 , 可以給予第二次機會 。 這是我的下一本書 。
it's inspiring . and it brings me to my last category of hope , and we've heard about this so much in the last two days: this indomitable human spirit . this determination of people , the resilience of the human spirit , so that people who you would think would be battered by poverty , or disease , or whatever , can pull themselves up out of it , sometimes with a helping hand , and take their part in society , and take their part in changing the world .	這很鼓舞人心 。 這帶給我最後一個希望的類別 , 我們在過去兩天裡都聽過這一點:這種不屈不撓的人類精神 。 這個決心 , 人類精神的韌性 , 使你認為會被貧窮、疾病所打擊的人們 , 或其他的人們 , 有時會用手伸出手 , 把他們的部分帶進社會中 , 改變世界 。
and just to think of one or two people out of africa who are just really inspiring .	想想非洲有一兩個人 , 他們真的很鼓舞人心 。
we could make a very long list , but obviously nelson mandela , emerging from 17 years of hard physical labor , 23 years of imprisonment , with this amazing ability to forgive , so that he could lead his nation out the evil regime of apartheid without a bloodbath .	我們可以列出很長的清單 , 但顯然納爾遜•曼德拉從十七年的辛苦勞動 , 23年的監禁 , 帶著這令人驚訝的寬恕的能力 , 讓他能帶領他的國家 , 走出種族隔離的邪惡政權 , 沒有血盆 。
ken sarowiwa , in nigeria , who took on the giant oil companies , and although people around the world tried their best , was executed .	奈及利亞的肯薩萊瓦 , 他接納了巨型石油公司 , 雖然全世界的人都嘗試了最好的 , 被處決了 。
people like this are so inspirational .	像這樣的人非常鼓舞人心 。
people like this are the role models we need for young africans .	像這樣的人 , 是非洲年輕人所需要的榜樣 。
and we need some environmental role models as well , and i've been hearing some of them today .	我們也需要一些環保的榜樣 , 我今天也聽過一些 。
so i'm really grateful for this opportunity to share this message again , with everyone at ted .	所以 , 我很感激這個機會再次分享這個訊息 , 和ted的每個人分享 。
and i hope that some of us can get together and talk about some of these things , especially the roots and shoots program .	我希望有些人能聚在一起討論這些事 , 特別是根與芽計畫 。
and just a last word on that the young woman who's running this entire conference center , i met her today .	最後一個詞是一位經營這整個會議中心的年輕女士 , 我今天認識了她 。
she came up so excited , with her certificate . she was [in] roots and shoots .	她很興奮 , 她的認證很興奮 。 她是根和芽 。
she was in the leadership in dar es salaam .	她在達拉姆的領導階層 。
she said it's helped her to do what she's doing .	她說 , 這協助她做她正在做的事 。
and it was very , very exciting for me to meet her and see just one example of how young people , when they are empowered , given the opportunity to take action , to make the world a better place , truly are our hope for tomorrow .	讓我非常興奮地見到她 , 看到一個例子 , 說明年輕人是如何被賦權的 , 因為有機會採取行動 , 讓世界變得更美好 , 真正是我們明天的希望 。
artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家黛安娜柯恩在海洋中和我們的生活中 , 分享了一些關於塑膠污染的艱難真相 。 還有一些想法 , 關於如何從塑膠健身中解放我們自己 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費主義、全球議題、綠色、使命藍、海洋、塑膠、塑膠等 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	黛安娜柯恩:對塑膠污染的艱難真相 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是視覺藝術家 , 我也是塑膠污染聯盟的共同創辦人之一 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我一直在研究塑膠袋 , 我把塑膠袋剪下來 , 縫合成我作品的主要材料 , 在過去二十年間 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們變成二維、三維空間的碎片、雕塑和裝置 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	在與塑膠合作的前八年 , 我的工作中 , 有些開始裂縫 , 分解成更小的塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 太棒了 。
it's ephemeral just like us . "	跟我們一樣是短暫的 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	在我更進一步教育塑膠時 , 我發現這是件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	塑膠會分解成更小的部分 , 因為它總是塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們發現 , 很多都是在海洋環境中 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	接著 , 在過去幾年 , 我學到太平洋垃圾堆和健身房 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	我最初的反應和我認為這是很多人對它的第一個反應: 「 天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們得要走出去 , 把這個東西清乾淨 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	因此我提出了一個提案 , 要搭乘貨櫃 , 和兩艘被丟棄的漁船拖船 , 一艘船 , 一台滑雪機器 , 和一台冷冰的機器 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	我的意圖是要走到健身房 , 提高對這個議題的認知 , 並開始將塑膠分解成一點點 , 將它冷到磚塊中 , 讓它可以被當作社區內部的建築材料 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和那些曾經去過健身房的人聊天 , 研究海洋環境裡的塑膠問題 , 我意識到 , 清理它會是非常小的一滴 , 相較於每天在世界各地產生的數量 , 實際上 , 我需要回頭看看更大的圖片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到一種方法來關掉水龍頭 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要切割使用和丟棄塑膠的位置 , 每天都要進入海洋環境 , 以全球性的規模 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	仔細看 , 我也了解到我真的很生氣 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只在乎塑膠 , 你在太平洋中期想出來 , 我發現現在有11個健身 , 可能是世界上五個大海裡的塑膠 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	我所關心的塑膠不僅僅是超市裡的塑膠工廠 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我會去超市 , 所有的食物都是塑膠包裝 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我所有的飲料都是塑膠的包裝 , 甚至在健康食品市場上 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也擔心冰箱裡的塑膠 , 我擔心塑膠和毒素會從塑膠中滲透到我們體內 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以我和一群人聚在一起 , 他們都在研究這個議題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染聯盟 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有很多我們正在努力的倡議 , 但其中有些是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	第一:如果80%到90%的海洋碎片 , 我們在海洋中發現的就是塑膠 , 那我們為什麼不把它稱之為 「 塑膠 」 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收每個人的書 , 都是關於永續發展和綠化 , 都是回收的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把東西放到一塊垃圾桶裡 , 你不用再想一想 。
what is the reality of that ?	這是什麼呢 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 低於7%的塑膠回收 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你仔細觀察 , 特別是塑膠瓶 , 大部份只會被低收利用 , 或被焚化 , 或運送到中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它的循環被轉換成比較少的東西 , 玻璃瓶可以再次變成玻璃瓶 , 或是再次使用塑膠瓶 , 絕對不會再次成為塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這對我們來說是個大問題 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另一件我們正在看的東西 , 請大家思考的是 , 我們在 「 減少、再利用、回收 」 前面加上了第四個r , 那就拒絕了 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	每當可能發生時 , 都會拒絕使用和丟棄的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代方案存在 ; 有些是很古老的 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在在收集這些冷酷的pyrex容器 , 用這些裝置 , 而不是發電裝置來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道我對自己和我的家人做了一個服務 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很容易就拿起不穩定的瓶子或玻璃瓶 , 如果你在旅行 , 你忘了把你的不穩定的瓶裝滿水或過濾水 , 和購買塑膠瓶裝水 。
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我想在座的各位 , 我知道你們對這個議題的了解是 , 這在海洋中是個大問題 , 但身為消費者 , 我們所創造出的問題是可以解決的 。
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們可以藉由提高意識到這個問題並教導人們選擇替代方案 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	所以每當可能時 , 選擇使用單一塑膠的替代方案 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們可以將它的幹細胞切成海洋 , 這樣一來 , 拯救海洋 , 拯救地球 , 拯救我們自己 。
this demo from pattie maes' lab at mit , spearheaded by pranav mistry was the buzz of ted . it's a wearable device with a projector that paves the way for profound interaction with our environment . imagine " minority report " and then some .	來自麻省理工學院的pattiemaes實驗室的示範 , 由pranavmitry所發表的 , 是ted的buzz 。 這是一個可穿戴式裝置 , 用投影機來繪製我們與環境的深度互動 。 想像一下 , 「 少數報告 」 再加上一些 。
demo , design , interface design , technology	demo , 設計 , 介面設計 , 科技 , 科技 。
pattie maes and pranav mistry demo sixthsense	pattiemaes和panav錯過了第六感 。
i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我對這個問題很感興趣 , 關於我們能否進化或發展出第六感的感覺 , 給予我們無縫接觸和容易取得的資訊 , 或可能存在的資訊 , 可以協助我們做出正確的決定 , 來決定我們要面對的是什麼 。
and some of you may argue , well , don't today's cell phones do that already ?	有些人可能會認為 , 今天的手機已經不行了嗎 ?
but i would say no .	但我會說 , 不 。
when you meet someone here at ted and this is the top networking place , of course , of the year you don't shake somebody's hand and then say , " can you hold on for a moment while i take out my phone and google you ? "	當你在ted認識一個人 , 當然 , 這是最頂尖的網絡場所 , 在那年你不會握手 , 然後說: 「 你能拿出我的手機和google嗎 ? 」
or when you go to the supermarket and you're standing there in that huge aisle of different types of toilet papers , you don't take out your cell phone , and open a browser , and go to a website to try to decide which of these different toilet papers is the most ecologically responsible purchase to make .	或當你去超市 , 你站在那一大堆不同的馬桶文件裡 , 你不會拿出你的手機 , 打開瀏覽器 , 去一個網站 , 試著決定這些不同的廁所論文是最環保的購買 。
so we don't really have easy access to all this relevant information that can just help us make optimal decisions about what to do next and what actions to take .	所以我們並不容易取得所有相關的資訊 , 只能協助我們做出最佳的決定 , 決定下一步該怎麼做 , 以及該採取什麼行動 。
and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以我在媒體實驗室的研究團隊開發了一系列的發明 , 讓我們能以一種簡單的方式取得這些資訊 , 而不需要使用者改變他們的行為 。
and i'm here to unveil our latest effort , and most successful effort so far , which is still very much a work in process .	我來這裡是為了揭開我們最新的努力 , 目前為止 , 最成功的努力 , 在過程中仍然是一份工作 。
i'm actually wearing the device right now and we've sort of cobbled it together with components that are off the shelf and that , by the way , only cost 350 dollars at this point in time .	我現在正戴著這個裝置 , 我們把它融合在一起 , 順帶一提 , 目前只需要花350美元 。
i'm wearing a camera , just a simple webcam , a portable , batterypowered projection system with a little mirror .	我戴著相機 , 只是一個簡單的網路攝影機 , 一個可攜式、電池驅動的投影系統 , 用鏡子 。
these components communicate to my cell phone in my pocket which acts as the communication and computation device .	這些元件跟我的口袋裡的手機溝通 , 它是溝通和計算裝置 。
and in the video here we see my student pranav mistry , who's really the genius who's been implementing and designing this whole system .	在影片中 , 我們看到我的學生帕納•錯誤 , 他真的是天才 , 他一直在執行和設計這整個系統 。
and we see how this system lets him walk up to any surface and start using his hands to interact with the information that is projected in front of him .	我們看到這個系統讓他走到任何表面 , 開始用他的雙手來和他面前投射的資訊互動 。
the system tracks the four significant fingers .	系統追蹤了四隻手指 。
in this case , he's wearing simple marker caps that you may recognize .	在這個案例中 , 他戴著你可能認得的簡單標記帽 。
but if you want a more stylish version you could also paint your nails in different colors .	但如果你想要更風格的版本 , 你也可以用不同顏色來畫你的指甲 。
and the camera basically tracks these four fingers and recognizes any gestures that he's making so he can just go to , for example , a map of long beach , zoom in and out , etc .	攝影機基本上追蹤這四隻手指並辨識出他所創造的任何手勢 , 例如 , 長灘的地圖 , 放大 , 等等 。
the system also recognizes iconic gestures such as the " take a picture " gesture , and then takes a picture of whatever is in front of you .	系統也能辨識出像 「 拍照 」 的標誌性姿勢 , 然後拍一張你面前的任何東西 。
and when he then walks back to the media lab , he can just go up to any wall and project all the pictures that he's taken , sort through them and organize them , and resize them , etc . , again using all natural gestures .	當他走回媒體實驗室時 , 他可以走到任何牆上 , 投射他拍攝的所有照片 , 把它們整理起來 , 再次重塑 , 再次使用所有自然的手勢 。
so , some of you most likely were here two years ago and saw the demo by jeff han or some of you may think , " well , doesn't this look like the microsoft surface table ? "	有些人可能在兩年前就在這裡看到傑夫•漢的示範 , 有些人可能會想: 「 嗯 , 這看起來不像微軟的表面桌子嗎 ? 」
and yes , you also interact using natural gestures , both hands , etc .	是的 , 你也會用自然的手勢來互動 , 雙手等等 。
but the difference here is that you can use any surface , you can walk to up to any surface , including your hand if nothing else is available and interact with this projected data .	但不同的是 , 你可以用任何表面 , 你可以走到任何表面 , 包括你的手 , 如果沒有其他東西可以用 , 和這個投影資料互動 。
the device is completely portable , and can be . . .	這個裝置是可攜式的 , 可以......
so one important difference is that it's totally mobile .	其中一個重要的差別是它完全是行動起來的 。
another even more important difference is that in mass production this would not cost more tomorrow than today's cell phones and would actually not sort of be a bigger packaging could look a lot more stylish than this version that i'm wearing around my neck .	另一個更重要的差別是 , 在大規模生產上 , 這不會比現今的手機花更多 , 也不會變成更大的包裝 , 看起來比我在脖子上戴的這個版本還要多 。
but other than letting some of you live out your fantasy of looking as cool as tom cruise in " minority report , " the reason why we're really excited about this device is that it really can act as one of these sixthsense devices that gives you relevant information about whatever is in front of you .	但除此之外 , 除了讓你們之外 , 在《少數報告》中的湯姆•克魯斯 , 我們之所以對這個裝置感到興奮的原因 , 是因為它真的可以扮演這第六感的裝置之一 , 讓你有相關資訊 , 讓你知道在你面前的任何東西 。
so we see pranav here going into the supermarket and he's shopping for some paper towels .	我們看到帕納走進超市 , 他正在購買一些紙巾 。
and , as he picks up a product the system can recognize the product that he's picking up , using either image recognition or marker technology , and give him the green light or an orange light .	當他拿起產品系統時 , 可以辨識出他所拿到的產品 , 用的是影像辨識或標記技術 , 給他綠光或橘色光 。
he can ask for additional information .	他可以要求額外的資訊 。
so this particular choice here is a particularly good choice , given his personal criteria .	所以這個特別的選擇 , 特別是他個人的標準 。
some of you may want the toilet paper with the most bleach in it rather than the most ecologicallyresponsible choice .	有些人可能希望廁所紙上有最多的白化紙 , 而不是最環保的選擇 。
if he picks up a book in the bookstore , he can get an amazon rating it gets projected right on the cover of the book .	如果他在書店裡拿起一本書 , 他可以拿到亞馬遜的評分 , 它就會被投射到書的封面上 。
this is juan's book , our previous speaker , which gets a great rating , by the way , at amazon .	這是胡安的書 , 我們先前的講者 , 順便說一下 , 在亞馬遜得到了很棒的評分 。
and so , pranav turns the page of the book and can then see additional information about the book reader comments , maybe sort of information by his favorite critic , etc .	所以 , 帕納翻了書的頁面 , 再看看書中讀者留言的額外資訊 , 可能是他最喜歡的批評 , 等等 。
if he turns to a particular page he finds an annotation by maybe an expert of a friend of ours that gives him a little bit of additional information about whatever is on that particular page .	如果他轉到特定的頁面 , 他可能找到了我們朋友的註解專家 , 給他一些關於那一頁內容的額外資訊 。
reading the newspaper it never has to be outdated .	閱讀報紙 , 它永遠不會被過時 。
you can get video annotations of the event that you're reading about you can get the latest sports scores etc .	你可以得到你正在讀的事件的影片註冊 , 你可以得到最新的體育分數 。
this is a more controversial one .	這是更具爭議性的 。
as you interact with someone at ted , maybe you can see a word cloud of the tags , the words that are associated with that person in their blog and personal web pages .	當你和ted的某人互動 , 也許你能看到標籤的雲 , 和那個人的部落格和個人網頁相關的字詞 。
in this case , the student is interested in cameras , etc .	在這個案例中 , 學生對攝影機有興趣 , 等等 。
on your way to the airport , if you pick up your boarding pass , it can tell you that your flight is delayed , that the gate has changed , etc .	在你去機場的路上 , 如果你拿起你的登機通行證 , 它可以告訴你你的航班延遲了 , 大門已經改變了 , 等等 。
and , if you need to know what the current time is it's as simple as drawing a watch on your arm .	如果你需要知道現在的時刻 , 就像在你的手臂上畫一支手臂上的手錶一樣簡單 。
so that's where we're at so far in developing this sixth sense that would give us seamless access to all this relevant information about the things that we may come across .	這就是我們目前正在發展的第六感 , 讓我們能取得所有關於我們可能遇到的事物的相關資訊 。
my student pranav , who's really , like i said , the genius behind this .	我的學生帕拉夫 , 真的 , 就像我說的 , 背後的天才 。
he does deserve a lot of applause because i don't think he's slept much in the last three months , actually .	他的確需要很多掌聲 , 因為我不認為他在過去三個月中睡得太多 。
and his girlfriend is probably not very happy about him either .	他的女友也可能對他也不滿意 。
but it's not perfect yet , it's very much a work in progress .	但它還不完美 , 它在進步中非常多 。
and who knows , maybe in another 10 years we'll be here with the ultimate sixth sense brain implant .	誰知道 , 或許在接下來的十年 , 我們將會與第六次的大腦植入 。
phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	菲利斯•羅德里格茲和艾ichaelwafi有一個強大的友誼 , 來自於無法想像的失去 。 羅德里格茲的兒子在世界貿易中心被殺害 , 2001年9月11日 , 伊爾威菲的兒子佐伊在那些攻擊中被判有一場角色 , 並且在這些攻擊中被判有生命的句子 。 希望找到和平 , 這兩位母親都能互相了解和尊重 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球議題、政治、政治、
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11癒合:那些找到寬恕、友誼的母親 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	菲利斯•羅德里格茲:我們今天在這裡是因為我們有大多數人認為非比尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 我們現在感覺很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我第一次了解到我兒子在世界貿易中心在2001年9月11日的早上 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他是否死了 , 直到36小時之後 。
at the time , we knew that it was political .	當時 , 我們知道它是政治性的 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們害怕我們的國家會怎麼做 , 以我們兒子的名字 , 我的丈夫 , 奧蘭多 , 我和我們的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它時 , 很震驚的是 , 我們的生命中糟糕的爆炸 , 真的 , 我們並沒有被復仇 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾個星期後 , zacariasmoussaoui被指控在六次犯下恐怖主義的陰謀上 , 以及美國政府要求為他死刑 , 如果定罪了 , 我的丈夫和我在公開對他說話 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過這些和人權團體 , 我們和許多其他受害者的家人聚在一起 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到艾妮莎 , 她兒子被指控 , 我心想: 「 什麼是勇敢的女人 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 當我更強壯的時候 , 我想要和那個女人見面 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我仍然在悲慟中 ; 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道我有一天會找到她 , 或我們會找到彼此 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為 , 當人們聽到我兒子是受害者時 , 我立刻得到同情 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們知道她的兒子被指控時 , 她沒有得到同情 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的苦難和我一樣 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	我們在2002年11月見面 , 艾icha現在會告訴你這是怎麼來的 。
aicha elwafi: good afternoon , ladies and gentlemen .	aichaelwafi:下午 , 各位先生女士 。
i am the mother of zacarias moussaoui .	我是zacariasmoussaui的母親 。
and i asked the organization of human rights to put me in touch with the parents of the victims .	我請人權組織讓我聯絡受害者的父母 。
so they introduced me to five families .	所以他們向我介紹五個家庭 。
and i saw phyllis , and i watched her .	我看到phyllis , 我看著她 。
she was the only mother in the group .	她是群體中唯一的母親 。
the others were brothers , sisters .	其他人則是兄弟姊妹 。
and i saw in her eyes that she was a mother , just like me .	我在她的眼中看到她就像我一樣 。
i suffered a lot as a mother .	我身為母親 , 遭受許多苦難 。
i was married when i was 14 .	我14歲時結婚 。
i lost a child when i was 15 , a second child when i was 16 .	我十五歲時失去了一個孩子 , 那時我十六歲 。
so the story with zacarias was too much really .	所以zacaria的故事實在太多了 。
and i still suffer , because my son is like he's buried alive .	我仍然受苦 , 因為我的兒子就像活著一樣 。
i know she really cried for her son .	我知道她真的為她的兒子哭了 。
but she knows where he is .	但她知道他在哪裡 。
my son , i don't know where he is .	我的兒子 , 我不知道他在哪裡 。
i don't know if he's alive . i don't know if he's tortured .	我不知道他是否活著 , 我不知道他是否受刑 。
i don't know what happened to him .	我不知道他發生了什麼事 。
so that's why i decided to tell my story , so that my suffering is something positive for other women .	所以 , 這就是為什麼我決定要說我的故事 , 所以我的痛苦對其他女性來說是正面的 。
for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	對於所有婦女 , 所有給予生命的媽媽 , 你可以回饋 , 你可以改變 。
it's up to us women , because we are women , because we love our children .	取決於我們女性 , 因為我們是女性 , 因為我們愛我們的孩子 。
we must be handinhand and do something together .	我們必須親手合作 。
it's not against women , it's for us , for us women , for our children .	不是反對女性 , 而是為了我們 , 為我們女性 , 為我們的孩子 。
i talk against violence , against terrorism .	我談到暴力 , 對抗恐怖主義 。
i go to schools to talk to young , muslim girls so they don't accept to be married against their will very young .	我去學校跟年輕的穆斯林女孩說話 , 這樣她們不接受婚姻會很年輕 。
so if i can save one of the young girls , and avoid that they get married and suffer as much as i did , well this is something good .	所以 , 如果我能拯救其中一位年輕女孩 , 避免她們結婚和受苦 , 嗯 , 這是件好事 。
this is why i'm here in front of you .	這就是為什麼我會站在你們面前 。
pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	pr:我想說 , 我從阿加哈學到很多 , 從那天起 , 我們第一次和其他家庭成員開會 , 那是一個非常私人的會議 , 因為那是2002年11月 , 而且 , 坦白說 , 我們害怕那個國家那個時候的超級病菌 。
but we were all so nervous .	但我們都非常緊張 。
" why does she want to meet us ? "	「 她為什麼要見我們 ? 」
and then she was nervous .	然後她緊張了 。
" why did we want to meet her ? "	「 為什麼我們要見她 ? 」
what did we want from each other ?	我們想要彼此的是什麼 ?
before we knew each others' names , or anything , we had embraced and wept .	在我們認識彼此的名字之前 , 或任何東西之前 , 我們都接受了和哭泣 。
then we sat in a circle with support , with help , from people experienced in this kind of reconciliation .	接著 , 我們坐在一個圓圈裡 , 帶著幫助 , 帶著幫助 , 從人們身上 , 體驗到這種和解 。
and aicha started , and she said , " i don't know if my son is guilty or innocent , but i want to tell you how sorry i am for what happened to your families .	aicha開始了 , 她說: 「 我不知道我的兒子是否有罪惡感或無辜 , 但我想告訴你 , 我對你的家人的狀況有多麼抱歉 。
i know what it is to suffer , and i feel that if there is a crime , a person should be tried fairly and punished . "	我知道要受苦的是什麼 , 我覺得如果有犯罪 , 一個人應該要被公平的審判和懲罰 。 」
but she reached out to us in that way , and it was , i'd like to say , it was an icebreaker .	但她用那樣的方式向我們伸出援手 , 我想要說 , 那是個冰桶 。
and what happened then is we all told our stories , and we all connected as human beings .	接下來發生的是 , 我們都說了我們的故事 , 我們都以人類的身分連結 。
by the end of the afternoon it was about three hours after lunch we'd felt as if we'd known each other forever .	下午就結束了 , 午餐後的三小時 , 我們感覺好像我們永遠認識彼此一樣 。
now what i learned from her , is a woman , not only who could be so generous under these present circumstances and what it was then , and what was being done to her son , but the life she's had .	我從她身上學到的 , 是女人 , 不僅僅是如此慷慨 , 在這些現況下 , 及當時的狀況下 , 以及她兒子所做的事 , 還有她所經歷的人生 。
i never had met someone with such a hard life , from such a totally different culture and environment from my own .	我從來沒有遇過像這樣艱難的生活 , 來自我自己的文化和環境 。
and i feel that we have a special connection , which i value very much .	我覺得我們有一個特別的連結 , 我非常重視 。
and i think it's all about being afraid of the other , but making that step and then realizing , " hey , this wasn't so hard .	我覺得這全是為了害怕另一個人 , 但要踏出那一步 , 然後意識到: 「 嘿 , 這一點也不難 。
who else can i meet that i don't know , or that i'm so different from ? "	我還能和誰見面 , 我不知道 , 或我和誰很不一樣 ? 」
so , aicha , do you have a couple of words for conclusion ?	所以 , aicha , 你有幾個字要做結論嗎 ?
because our time is up .	因為我們的時間到了 。
aw: i wanted to say that we have to try to know other people , the other .	aw:我想說 , 我們必須試著認識別人 , 其他人 。
you have to be generous , and your hearts must be generous , your mind must be generous .	你必須慷慨 , 你的心一定是慷慨的 , 你的心靈一定是慷慨的 。
you must be tolerant .	你一定是包容的 。
you have to fight against violence .	你必須對抗暴力 。
and i hope that someday we'll all live together in peace and respecting each other .	我希望有一天我們都能一起生活在和平中 , 互相尊重 。
this is what i wanted to say .	這是我想要說的 。
too much of the world lacks access to clean drinking water . engineer michael pritchard did something about it inventing the portable lifesaver filter , which can make the most revolting water drinkable in seconds . an amazing demo from tedglobal 2009 .	太多世界缺乏乾淨飲用水的管道 。 工程師麥可•普立特在發明可攜式的救命過濾器 , 可以在幾秒鐘內完成最適合飲用水的示範 。 這是2009年tedglobal的驚人示範 。

i'd like to talk about a couple of things today .	今天我想談談幾件事 。
the first thing is water .	第一件事是水 。
now i see you've all been enjoying the water that's been provided for you here at the conference , over the past couple of days .	現在我看到你們都很享受在研討會上為你們提供的水 , 在過去幾天裡 。
and i'm sure you'll feel that it's from a safe source .	我相信你們會覺得這是安全的來源 。
but what if it wasn't ?	但如果不是呢 ?
what if it was from a source like this ?	如果它是來自這樣的來源呢 ?
then statistics would actually say that half of you would now be suffering with diarrhea .	接著 , 統計數字會說你們當中一半的人現在會遭受腹瀉的苦難 。
i talked a lot in the past about statistics , and the provision of safe drinking water for all .	我在過去談了很多關於統計的議題 , 以及為所有人提供安全飲用水的條件 。
but they just don't seem to get through .	但他們似乎不會穿透 。
and i think i've worked out why .	我想我已經找出原因了 。
it's because , using current thinking , the scale of the problem just seems too huge to contemplate solving .	因為 , 使用目前的思考 , 問題的規模似乎太大了 , 無法解決 。
so we just switch off: us , governments and aid agencies .	所以我們就關掉了:我們、政府和援助機構 。
well , today , i'd like to show you that through thinking differently , the problem has been solved .	今天 , 我想用不同的方式來告訴各位 , 問題已經解決了 。
by the way , since i've been speaking , another 13 , 000 people around the world are suffering now with diarrhea .	順道一提 , 自從我開始演講之後 , 世界各地有一萬三千人正在受腹瀉所苦 。
and four children have just died .	四個孩子剛過世了 。
i invented lifesaver bottle because i got angry .	我發明了生命安全瓶 , 因為我生氣了 。
i , like most of you , was sitting down , the day after christmas in 2004 , when i was watching the devastating news of the asian tsunami as it rolled in , playing out on tv .	我和你們大部分人一樣 , 在2004年聖誕節過後的那天 , 當我在看亞洲海嘯的消息 , 當它滾進來時 , 我在電視上演出 。
the days and weeks that followed , people fleeing to the hills , being forced to drink contaminated water or face death .	接下來的日子和幾週 , 人們逃到山丘上 , 被迫喝下受污染的水或死亡 。
that really stuck with me .	這真的困擾了我 。
then , a few months later , hurricane katrina slammed into the side of america .	然後 , 幾個月後 , 颶風卡崔娜衝進美國邊 。
" okay , " i thought , " here's a first world country , let's see what they can do . "	「 好吧 , 」 我想: 「 這是第一個世界國家 , 咱們來看看他們能做什麼 。 」
do you know it took five days to get water to the superdome ?	你知道要花五天才能把水送到超級名嗎 ?
people were shooting each other on the streets for tv sets and water .	人們在街上為電視設定和水拍攝彼此 。
that's when i decided i had to do something .	那是我決定要做點什麼的時候 。
now i spent a lot of time in my garage , over the next weeks and months , and also in my kitchen much to the dismay of my wife .	現在我花了很多時間在我的車庫裡 , 在接下來的幾週、幾個月 , 在我的廚房裡 , 我太太太很不滿 。
however , after a few failed prototypes , i finally came up with this , the lifesaver bottle .	然而 , 在幾次失敗的原型之後 , 我終於想到了這個 , 救命瓶 。
okay , now for the science bit .	好 , 現在來談科學 。
before lifesaver , the best hand filters were only capable of filtering down to about 200 nanometers .	在生物救世代之前 , 最好的手過濾器只能過濾大約200奈米 。
the smallest bacteria is about 200 nanometers .	最小的細菌大約是200奈米 。
so a 200nanometer bacteria is going to get through a 200nanometer hole .	所以一個200奈米的細菌將會穿過一個200奈米的洞 。
the smallest virus , on the other hand , is about 25 nanometers .	另一方面 , 最小的病毒大約是25奈米 。
so that's definitely going to get through those 200 nanometer holes .	這絕對是要穿過200奈米的洞 。
lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	救命者池塘是15奈米 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 沒有任何東西能穿過 。
okay , i'm going to give you a bit of a demonstration .	好 , 我來示範一下 。
would you like to see that ?	你們想看到嗎 ?
i spent all the time setting this up , so i guess i should .	我花了很多時間把這些設定好 , 我想我應該這樣做 。
we're in the fine city of oxford .	我們在牛津的最好城市 。
so someone's done that up .	有人這樣做 。
fine city of oxford , so what i've done is i've gone and got some water from the river cherwell , and the river thames , that flow through here . and this is the water .	美好的牛津城 , 所以我做的是 , 我從河流中取得一些水 , 河流的thames , 流過這裡 。 這就是水 。
but i got to thinking , you know , if we were in the middle of a flood zone in bangladesh , the water wouldn't look like this .	但我想 , 如果我們在孟加拉的洪水區中央 , 水不會像這樣 。
so i've gone and got some stuff to add into it .	所以 , 我做了一些東西來加入它 。
and this is from my pond .	這是我的池塘 。
have a smell of that , mister cameraman .	聞一下 , 攝影師先生 。
we're just going to pour that in there .	我們只會把它倒進去 。
michael pritchard: okay . we've got some runoff from a sewage plant farm .	michaelpritchard:好的 , 我們有一些從污水廠運來的 。
so i'm just going to put that in there .	所以 , 我要把它放進去 。
put that in there . there we go .	把它放進去 , 就這樣 。
and some other bits and pieces , chuck that in there .	其他的碎片和碎片 。

so we're just going to put that in there as well .	我們也要把它放進去 。
the lifesaver bottle works really simply .	救生員的瓶子很簡單 。
you just scoop the water up .	你只是把水往上跑 。
today i'm going to use a jug just to show you all . let's get a bit of that poo in there .	今天我要用一個評斷來給你們看 。 讓我們看看裡面的一些小馬 。
that's not dirty enough . let's just stir that up a little bit .	這還不夠髒 。 讓我們稍微攪拌一下 。
okay , so i'm going to take this really filthy water , and put it in here . do you want a drink yet ?	好 , 我要把這個非常骯髒的水放進這裡 , 你還想喝杯嗎 ?
okay . there we go .	好了 , 開始了 。
give it a few pumps . okay ?	給它一些幫浦 。 好嗎 ?
that's all that's necessary .	那是必要的 。
now as soon as i pop the teat , sterile drinking water is going to come out .	一旦我打開了茶 , 無菌的飲用水就會出現 。
i've got to be quick . okay , ready ?	我得很快 , 準備好了嗎 ?
there we go . mind the electrics .	來了 , 注意一下電 。
that is safe , sterile drinking water .	那是安全、無菌的飲用水 。
there you go chris .	來吧克里斯 。
what's it taste of ?	它有什麼味道 ?
let's see chris's program throughout the rest of the show . okay ?	我們來看看克里斯在其餘的節目 。 好嗎 ?
okay . lifesaver bottle is used by thousands of people around the world .	好 , 世界各地數以千計的人使用了救命瓶 。
it'll last for 6 , 000 liters .	它會維持6 , 000公升 。
and when it's expired , using failsafe technology , the system will shut off , protecting the user .	用失敗的技術 , 系統會關閉 , 保護使用者 。
pop the cartridge out . pop a new one in .	把車禍趕出去 , 打開一個新進去 。
it's good for another 6 , 000 liters .	對6 , 000公升來說是好的 。
so let's look at the applications .	咱們來看看應用程式 。
traditionally , in a crisis , what do we do ?	傳統上 , 在危機中 , 我們該怎麼做 ?
then , after a few weeks , we set up camps .	幾週後 , 我們成立了營地 。
and people are forced to come into the camps to get their safe drinking water .	人們被迫進入營地 , 以取得安全的飲用水 。
what happens when 20 , 000 people congregate in a camp ?	當兩萬人聚集在營地時 , 會發生什麼事 ?
diseases spread . more resources are required .	疾病散播 。 需要更多資源 。
the problem just becomes selfperpetuating .	問題就在於自我繁殖 。
but by thinking differently , and shipping these , people can stay put .	但藉由不同的思考 , 運送這些東西 , 人們可以留在上面 。
they can make their own sterile drinking water , and start to get on with rebuilding their homes and their lives .	他們可以自己製造無菌飲用水 , 開始重建家園和生活 。
now , it doesn't require a natural disaster for this to work .	現在 , 這並不需要天然災害才能運作 。
using the old thinking , of national infrastructure and pipe work , is too expensive .	使用舊的想法 , 國家基礎建設和管道工作太貴了 。
when you run the numbers on a calculator , you run out of noughts .	當你在計算機上運算時 , 你就沒有了 。
so here is the " thinking different " bit .	這裡有 「 思考不同 」 的部分 。
instead of shipping water , and using manmade processes to do it , let's use mother nature . she's got a fantastic system .	與其運送水 , 使用人造流程來做 , 讓我們用大自然 。 她有一個很棒的系統 。
she picks the water up from there , desalinates it , for free , transports it over there , and dumps it onto the mountains , rivers , and streams .	她從那裡撿起水 , 免費將水淡化 , 運送到那裡 , 把它丟到山上 , 河流 , 河流 。
and where do people live ? near water .	人們住在哪裡 ? 附近的水 。
all we've go to do is make it sterile . how do we do that ?	我們要做的就是讓它變得無菌 。 我們要怎麼做 ?
well , we could use the lifesaver bottle .	嗯 , 我們可以用救命奶瓶 。
or we could use one of these .	或者我們可以用其中一種 。
the same technology , in a jerry can .	同樣的技術 , 在傑利可以 。
this will process 25 , 000 liters of water ; that's good enough for a family of four , for three years .	這會處理2萬5千公升的水 ; 這足夠給四個家庭 , 三年之久 。
and how much does it cost ?	要花多少錢 ?
about half a cent a day to run .	一天要花半分錢跑 。
so , by thinking differently , and processing water at the point of use , mothers and children no longer have to walk four hours a day to collect their water .	所以 , 透過不同的思考方式 , 在使用的同時 , 母親和孩子們不再需要每天走四個小時來收集他們的水 。
they can get it from a source nearby .	他們可以從附近的來源取得它 。
so with just eight billion dollars , we can hit the millennium goal's target of halving the number of people without access to safe drinking water .	所以 , 只要花八十億美金 , 我們就能達到千禧目標 , 目標是要在沒有安全飲用水的情況下 , 把人數減少 。
to put that into context , the u . k . government spends about 12 billion pounds a year on foreign aid .	要把這些數據歸納為背景 , 英國政府每年要花大約一百二十億英鎊在外國援助上 。
but why stop there ?	但為什麼要停在那裡 ?
with 20 billion dollars , everyone can have access to safe drinking water .	有了20億美金 , 每個人都能取得安全飲用水 。
so the threeandahalf billion people that suffer every year as a result , and the two million kids that die every year , will live .	因此 , 每年有三百五十億人遭受苦難 , 每年有兩百萬名兒童死去 , 會活下來 。
paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	paddyashown聲稱我們現在生活在歷史上 , 權力正在改變它從來沒有的方式 。 在tedxbrussel的演講中 , 他將他所看到的3大全球轉變排列出來 。
foreign policy , global issues , politics , world cultures	外交政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化、文化、文化、
paddy ashdown: the global power shift	padyashown:全球權力轉移 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末 , 有一首非常有名的英文詩人寫的詩 。
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	據說 , 在1930年代 , 教堂的大腦迴響 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	這首詩是: 「 在夏天的伊德爾山丘上 , 帶著溪流的懶惰 , 哈克我聽到一個遙遠的鼓聲 , 像在夢裡的聲音 , 遙遠又低又大聲地在地球的道路上 , 親愛的朋友和食物到粉末 , 士兵遊行 , 很快就死了 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	那些對詩感興趣的人 , 這首詩是《shropshirelad》 , 由a.housman所寫 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但housman知道的 , 你也聽到尼爾森交響樂中 , 聽到的是19世紀長、炎熱、西爾文夏天的穩定性 , 即將到達一個近距離 , 而當權力改變時 , 我們將要進入一個可怕的時期 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	這些經期 , 各位先生女士 , 經常伴隨著亂流 , 經常被血液吸引 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	而我要告訴你們的訊息是 , 我相信我們被譴責 , 如果你喜歡 , 生活在歷史上的那些時刻之一 , 那時 , 權力的基礎已經開始改變 , 世界的新力量 , 已經開始形成 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	今天我們很清楚地看到 , 幾乎總是高頻繁、極度困難的時光 , 常常是非常血腥的時代 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順便一提 , 它每一世紀都會發生一次 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會認為 , 最後一次發生了 , 休斯曼的感覺也來了 , 教堂的感覺也一樣 , 當權力從舊國家傳遞時 , 歐洲的舊勢力 , 跨越大西洋 , 到美國新興的力量 , 美國剛開始 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在過去的歐洲權力過時的真空中 , 在上個世紀的兩個血腥災難中 , 第一部分和第二部分是:兩次世界大戰 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	毛澤東曾經稱他們為歐洲內戰 , 可能是更正確的描述方式 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	女士們先生們 , 我們生活在其中一次 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我今天要談三個因素 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	首先 , 這兩者的前兩項重點是權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於一些新的維度我想提一下 , 這從來沒有發生過 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但讓我們來談談權力的轉變 , 發生在世界上 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天發生的事 , 在某種意義上 , 很恐怖 , 因為它從來沒有發生過 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	我們已經看到希臘後來的權力轉移 , 在歐洲文明時期 , 羅馬和權力轉移的力量 , 但我們看到的有點不同 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不只是從國家延續到國家 。
it's also moving vertically .	它的垂直移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	現今正在發生的是 , 被監禁的權力 , 被監禁 , 被監禁在法律的規則上 , 在國家的制度中 , 現在已經大幅地移民到全球舞台上 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	我們談到全球化的權力 , 其實是真正的權力 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在國家的層面 , 權力被迫要負責法律的法則 , 在國際舞台上 , 權力並非如此 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際舞台和全球舞台現在有權力:網際網路的力量、衛星廣播的力量 , 貨幣的力量改變了這個廣大的金錢運輸工具 , 該交易的金額現在是32倍 , 該有金錢可以供應給金錢改變者 , 假如你喜歡 , 金融推測者 , 最近我們都帶給我們所有的財務推動者的力量 , 如今 , 跨國企業的預算能力 , 經常比發展中國家更大 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個幾乎沒有規範的全球空間 , 而非受到法律規範的影響 , 而在這樣的環境下 , 人們可能沒有限制 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	這套裝置強大到一瞬間 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	總是適合那些在沒有限制的空間中運作最有權力的人 , 但歷史的教訓是 , 很快地 , 沒有規範的空間不受法律規範的影響 , 不只是你想要的國際貿易、網路等等 。 還有你不想要的國際犯罪、國際恐怖主義的事 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件的啟示是 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 儘管如此 , 那些住在那空間的人 , 甚至可以在九月早上攻擊你最具代表性的城市 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	據說 , 被帶到911事件的四百萬美金中 , 大約有60%通過雙胞胎大樓的機構 , 911事件摧毀了 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	我們的敵人也用這個空間 , 大眾旅行、網路、衛星廣播家 , 來繞過毒藥 , 重點在於摧毀我們的系統和我們的方式 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	很快的 , 不久後 , 歷史的規則就是權力統治的目的必須跟隨著 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	所以 , 正如我所說的 , 正如我所說的 , 我們這個時代的一個現象就是全球化的權力 , 那麼我們這個時代所面臨的挑戰之一就是把治理帶到全球空間 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 未來的幾十年 , 將會是更大或更少的亂流 , 我們能達成這個目標:把治理帶到全球空間 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	注意 , 我不是在說政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是在說建立一些全球民主制度 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	順帶一提 , 我自己的觀點是 , 女士們先生們 , 女士們 , 女士們 , 不太可能透過擴展聯合國機構來做 。
if we didn't have the u . n . , we'd have to invent it .	如果我們沒有聯合國 , 我們就得發明它 。
the world needs an international forum .	世界需要一個國際論壇 。
it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要合法化的國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但 , 談到全球空間的治理 , 我猜 , 這不會發生在聯合國機構的創作中 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	事實上 , 強大的力量會聚集在一起 , 創造出以合約為基礎的系統 , 合約的協議 , 來管理這個全球空間 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到它們正在發生 , 已經開始出現了 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:以條約為基礎的組織 , 完全以合約為基礎 , 但 , 強大到能容納最強大的美國 , 如果有必要的話 。
kyoto: the beginnings of struggling to create a treatybased organization .	kyoto:努力創造一個合約的組織的開端 。
the g20: we know now that we have to put together an institution which is capable of bringing governance to that financial space for financial speculation .	g20:我們現在知道 , 我們得要組成一個機構 , 能夠把治理帶到金融空間 , 給金融推測 。
and that's what the g20 is , a treatybased institution .	而這就是g20 , 一個以條約為基礎的機構 。
now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	現在有個問題 , 我們等一下會再回來談 , 如果你把最強大的力量聚集在一起 , 以合約為基礎的機構制定規則 , 填補政府的空間 , 那弱者又會怎麼樣 ?
and that's a big problem , and we'll return to it in just a second .	這是個很大的問題 , 我們只要一秒鐘就能回報 。
so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你要傳遞這些亂流的次數 , 那麼 , 我們的成功程度就大程度上 , 取決於我們的能力 , 把合理的治理帶到全球空間 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看著這開始發生 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二點是 , 我知道我不需要和觀眾談談這種事 , 但權力不只是垂直轉移 , 它也在地平線轉移 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會認為 , 文明的歷史 , 已經被文明聚集在海洋周圍 , 聚集在地中海 , 最近在西方大西洋的力量中越是近期 。
well it seems to me that we're now seeing a fundamental shift of power , broadly speaking , away from nations gathered around the atlantic [seaboard] to the nations gathered around the pacific rim .	對我來說 , 我們現在看到的是權力的轉變 , 廣泛地說 , 遠離大西洋棋的國家聚集在太平洋邊緣的國家 。
now that begins with economic power , but that's the way it always begins .	這從經濟力量開始 , 但這一直是這樣開始的 。
you already begin to see the development of foreign policies , the augmentation of military budgets occurring in the other growing powers in the world .	你已經開始看到外交政策的發展 , 軍事預算的擴增發生在世界上其他增長的力量 。
i think actually this is not so much a shift from the west to the east ; something different is happening .	我認為 , 其實這不是西方的轉變 , 從東邊轉移到東邊 , 有些不同的事情正在發生 。
my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 美國在未來十年、15年 , 仍然是地球上最強大的國家 , 但她握有權力的情境現在已經徹底改變了 , 徹底改變了 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從50年來 , 最不尋常的歷史 , 到目前為止 , 我們有一個完全獨立的世界 , 在這個世界中 , 每個羅馬人所需要或對抗的同理心都必須被它的位置所指示 , 一個由一個巨人所組成的世界中 , 一個最好的世界 。
but that's not a usual case in history .	但這不是歷史上常見的案例 。
in fact , what's now emerging is the much more normal case of history .	事實上 , 現在出現的是更正常的歷史案例 。
you're beginning to see the emergence of a multipolar world .	你開始看到一個多極化的世界的出現 。
up until now , the united states has been the dominant feature of our world .	到目前為止 , 美國一直是我們世界的主流特徵 。
they will remain the most powerful nation , but they will be the most powerful nation in an increasingly multipolar world .	它們會維持最強大的國家 , 但它們會是越來越多極化的世界中最強大的國家 。
and you begin to see the alternative centers of power building up in china , of course , though my own guess is that china's ascent to greatness is not smooth .	你開始看到中國的權力建設中心 , 當然 , 我自己的猜測是中國的高興不是平滑的 。
it's going to be quite grumpy as china begins to democratize her society after liberalizing her economy .	當中國在自由化經濟後 , 將開始民主化她的社會 。
but that's a subject of a different discussion .	但這是另一個討論的主題 。
you see india , you see brazil .	你看到印度 , 巴西 。
you see increasingly that the world now looks actually , for us europeans , much more like europe in the 19th century .	你可以看到這個世界現在看起來 , 對我們歐洲人來說 , 更像19世紀的歐洲人 。
europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	十九世紀 , 歐洲 , 一位偉大的英國外交部長 , 總統 , 曾經把它描述為 「 歐洲的權力協會 」 。
there was a balance , a fivesided balance .	有一個平衡 , 一個五面體的平衡 。
britain always played to the balance .	英國總是為了平衡而演奏 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林合作 , 英國和維也納和羅馬合作 , 來提供平衡 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	請注意 , 在一個由單一世界主導的時期 , 你已經修復了聯盟 , 美國大陸公約組織 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	固定的權力兩極代表固定的盟友 。
but a multiple polarity of power means shifting and changing alliances .	但多重權力的兩極化意味著改變和改變盟友 。
and that's the world we're coming into , in which we will increasingly see that our alliances are not fixed .	這就是我們正在進入的世界 , 我們會漸漸看到我們的聯盟並沒有固定 。
canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	坎寧 , 偉大的英國秘書曾說過: 「 英國有共同的利益 , 但沒有共同盟友 。 」
and we will see increasingly that even we in the west will reach out , have to reach out , beyond the cozy circle of the atlantic powers to make alliances with others if we want to get things done in the world .	我們會發現 , 即使我們西方國家會伸出援手 , 還得伸出援手 , 超越大西洋力量的舒適圈 , 來和其他人聯盟 , 如果我們想讓世界上的一切做好 。
note , that when we went into libya , it was not good enough for the west to do it alone ; we had to bring others in .	注意 , 當我們進入利比亞時 , 西方的做法不夠好 ; 我們得要把他人帶進來 。
we had to bring , in this case , the arab league in .	在這個例子中 , 我們得帶入阿拉伯聯盟 。
my guess is iraq and afghanistan are the last times when the west has tried to do it themselves , and we haven't succeeded .	我的猜測是伊拉克和阿富汗是西方試圖自己做這件事的最後一次 , 我們還沒成功 。
my guess is that we're reaching the beginning of the end of 400 years i say 400 years because it's the end of the ottoman empire of the hegemony of western power , western institutions and western values .	我的猜測是400年底我說這是奧圖曼帝國結束西方勢力、西方制度和西方價值觀的終結
you know , up until now , if the west got its act together , it could propose and dispose in every corner of the world .	你知道 , 直到現在 , 如果西方國家團結起來 , 它可以在世界的各個角落提出並消除 。
but that's no longer true .	但這已經不是事實了 。
take the last financial crisis after the second world war .	以第二次世界大戰後最後的金融危機為例 。
the west got together the bretton woods institution , world bank , international monetary fund the problem solved .	西方國家聚集了布雷頓森林機構 , 世界銀行 , 國際貨幣基金會 , 解決了問題 。
now we have to call in others .	現在我們必須打電話給別人 。
now we have to create the g20 .	現在我們必須創造g20 。
now we have to reach beyond the cozy circle of our western friends .	現在我們要超越西方朋友的舒適圈 。
let me make a prediction for you , which is probably even more startling .	讓我為各位做個預測 , 這可能更令人驚訝 。
i suspect we are now reaching the end of 400 years when western power was enough .	我猜我們現在已經到了400年了 , 西方勢力已經足夠了 。
people say to me , " the chinese , of course , they'll never get themselves involved in peacemaking , multilateral peacemaking around the world . "	人們對我說: 「 中國人 , 當然 , 他們永遠不會參與到和平協調 , 全世界的多邊和平調停 。 」
oh yes ? why not ?	喔 ? 為什麼不呢 ?
how many chinese troops are serving under the blue beret , serving under the blue flag , serving under the u . n . command in the world today ?	有多少中國軍隊在藍色的貝雷特下服役 , 在藍旗下服役 , 在聯合國指揮下服役 ?
how many americans ? 11 .	有多少美國人 ? 11 。
what is the largest naval contingent tackling the issue of somali pirates ?	什麼是最大的海軍陸戰隊處理索馬利海盜議題 ?
the chinese naval contingent .	中國海軍總裁 。
of course they are , they are a mercantilist nation .	當然 , 他們是商業化的國家 。
they want to keep the sea lanes open .	他們想要保持海道開放 。
increasingly , we are going to have to do business with people with whom we do not share values , but with whom , for the moment , we share common interests .	漸漸地 , 我們得要和那些沒有共享價值的人做生意 , 但 , 在當下 , 我們有共同的利益 。
it's a whole new different way of looking at the world that is now emerging .	這是一種全新的看世界的方式 , 正在興起 。
and here's the third factor , which is totally different .	第三個因素 , 完全不同 。
today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	現今 , 在我們的現代世界裡 , 由於網路 , 因為人們在這裡所談論的東西 , 所有東西都和一切連結在一起 。
we are now interdependent .	我們現在是互相依賴的 。
we are now interlocked , as nations , as individuals , in a way which has never been the case before , never been the case before .	我們現在是相互關聯的 , 作為一個國家 , 作為個體 , 在某種程度上從來沒有發生過 , 從來沒有發生過 。
the interrelationship of nations , well it's always existed .	國家的相互關係 , 總是存在 。
diplomacy is about managing the interrelationship of nations .	外交是要管理國家的相互關係 。
but now we are intimately locked together .	但現在我們密切關在一起 。
you get swine flu in mexico , it's a problem for charles de gaulle airport 24 hours later .	你在墨西哥得到豬流感 , 二十四小時後查爾斯德高爾機場的問題 。
lehman brothers goes down , the whole lot collapses .	雷曼兄弟會下降 , 很多崩潰 。
there are fires in the steppes of russia , food riots in africa .	俄羅斯的步伐中有火災 , 非洲的食物暴動 。
we are all now deeply , deeply , deeply interconnected .	我們現在都深切、深切地相互連結 。
and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	這意味著 , 一個國家單獨行動 , 和他人連結 , 而不是和他人合作 , 不再是一個可行的提案 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為國家的動作既不被限制 , 也不足以控制國家本身 , 來控制自己的領土 , 因為國家之外的影響已經開始影響他們 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是英國帝國戰爭的年輕士兵 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	那時 , 我國家的辯護是一件事 , 只有一件事:我們的軍隊有多堅強 , 我們的空軍有多強大 , 我們的海軍有多強 , 我們的盟友有多強壯 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	那是敵人在牆外的時候 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人在牆壁裡 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	現在 , 如果我想要談談我國家的防禦 , 我得要和健康部談談 , 因為流行病對我的安全是威脅 , 我得要和農業部談談 , 因為食物安全是對我安全的威脅 , 我得要和產業的部長談談談 , 因為 , 我們希臘基礎建設的脆弱是對我們的敵人 , 從網路戰爭到我所見到的敵人 , 因為在我國家的房子裡 , 我們的家裡 , 已經有7個衝擊 , 因為在我的家裡 , 和7個房子裡 , 和7個房子裡 , 和7個房子裡的房子裡的家裡的家裡的家裡 , 和7個房子 。
